  <script>
   jQuery(function() {
	    // Unveil images 
	    var $images = jQuery("picture").find("source, img");
	    $images.unveil(200);
	    
	 	// Unveil widgets
	    var $widgets = jQuery(".lazy_widget");
	    $widgets.unveil(200, unveilWidget);
	    function unveilWidget() {
	    	var $this = jQuery(this);
	    	$.ajax({
	    		 url: $this.data("src"),
	    		 success: function( data ) {
	    			 var $newNode = $(data);
	    			 $this.replaceWith( $newNode );
	    			 jQuery( "source, img", $newNode ).unveil(200);
	    		 }
	    	});
	    }
	});
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function makeCRETrackingCall() {
				if (typeof cre_client !== 'undefined') {
				    cre_client.set_page_view();
				    cre_client.set_origin('web');
				    cre_client.set_service_id('shz');
				    cre_client.set_site('www.shz.de');
				    cre_client.set_content_id('/');
				    cre_client.set_cms_id('1');
				    cre_client.set_channel('1');
				    
				    cre_client.set_doc_type('section');
				    
				    cre_client.set_heading('Home');
				    
				    
				    cre_client.addListener(function(response) {
				    	if (response.data) {
				    		c1Response = response.data;
				    		_SHZ['userStatus'] = response.data.user_status;
				    	}
				    });
				    
				    cre_client.request();
				} else {
				    setTimeout(makeCRETrackingCall, 1000);
				}
			}
			makeCRETrackingCall();
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getTimeToFirstPaintIfSupported(){if(window.performance&&window.performance.timing){var c,a=window.performance.timing,b=a.navigationStart;if(window.chrome&&window.chrome.loadTimes?c=1e3*window.chrome.loadTimes().firstPaintTime:a.msFirstPaint&&(c=a.msFirstPaint),c&&b)return c-b}};
		var timeToFirstPaint = getTimeToFirstPaintIfSupported();

		jQuery(window).load(function() {
			if (typeof MSOdataLayer !== "undefined" && timeToFirstPaint) {
			   console.log('first paint:' + timeToFirstPaint);
			   MSOdataLayer.push({'event':'staticEvent', 'category':'Performance', 'action':'firstpaint', 'label':window.location.href , 'value':Math.round(timeToFirstPaint), 'interaction': 'false'});
			}
		});
  </script>
  <script>
   // Execute all encapsulated JS in window.requireObj as require.js is not part of this
			// release version, but JS in Code-Widgets is partly encapsulated in require() functions
			(function () {
				// Requirement to resource mapping
				var requirementsMap = {
					"$": jQuery  !== "undefined" ? jQuery : undefined,
					"jquery": jQuery !== "undefined" ? jQuery : undefined,
					"swfobject": swfobject  !== "undefined" ? swfobject : undefined
					// Weitere Ressourcen hier eintragen
				};
				// Execute all require() callbacks like require.js would do
				window.require = function (requirements, callback) {
					var allArgs = [];
					for(var r = 0, len = requirements.length; r < len; r++) {
						allArgs.push(requirementsMap[requirements[r]]);
					}
					callback.apply(this, allArgs);
				};
				// Execute all anonymous functions stored in requireObj
				for(var r = 0, len = requireObj.length; r < len; r++) {
					requireObj[r].apply();
				}
				
			})();
  </script>
